# Gift Card Merchant Candidate List - 5,000

This is a working candidate list for expanding BudgetBuddy gift-card merchant metadata. It is not shipped as the app autocomplete bundle yet.

- Target count: 5,000
- Current count: 5,000
- Source basis: OpenStreetMap Name Suggestion Index public brand/operator data
- Source URL: https://github.com/osmlab/name-suggestion-index
- Source license: BSD 3-Clause, copyright name-suggestion-index contributors
- Privacy rule: future app lookup must still download the full bundle and search locally only
- Quality rule: entries still need review before being treated as verified gift-card issuers
